<user>117417319259273041235<//user><Name>Gregory Tada<//Name><date>1543113086572<//date>< rate>
5< /rate>
< Review>
To some of the previous reviewers: FFS it's not ramen, okay? Don't expect tonkotsu broth. It's UDON.

I just ate here with the family and enjoyed it. There aren't many udon shops around here, and I was pleasantly surprised to find this in the mall. The broth was flavorful without being overpowering, and the noodles had nice body to them. I had the tempura udon, and while the shrimp was good the potato was a bit hard. Overall it's solid.

I'd usually give this place four stars, but I felt it necessary to offset the lame reviewers expecting ramen.< /Review>

< text>
Tsurumaru is located in the Eat area of the Santa Anita mall, next to Uncle Tetsu Cheesecake. The cashier mentioned that the shrimp tempura udon was a popular favorite, which also happens to be one of the most expensive items in the menu. I did end up ordering the tempura udon.

Upon receiving my entree, the tempura was over fried and dripping with oil. I peeled off the batter and just ate the shrimp and sweet potato. The udon was just ok, nothing special, but wasn't too horrible. However, the broth was super salty. I couldn't get rid of that saltiness after taste for the rest of the day.

Self serve type place where you get your own utensils and bus your own trays. Needless to say, I won't be returning.<//text>

<rating>5< /rating><text>Nella Terra is our GO-TO wine venue whenever we have out of town guests or friends we'd like to introduce to this gem of a setting, or if we'd just like to spend an afternoon tasting fine wines surrounded by the beauty that is Nella Terra.

As Wine Club members we've been treated to seasonal harvest or launch celebrations which have included live music and delicious food pairings provided by their caterer On the Vine. We've also enjoyed their Mother's Day Brunch and were thrilled they' offered  professional photo sessions all arranged by the Nella Terra staff. I'm so looking forward to the day these celebrations can resume.

I also look forward to postings by Nella Terra on Instagram of upcoming  weddings. I was fortunate to attend a Nella Terra wedding when friends of ours  gave their daughter the wedding of her dreams. I must say that it was absolutely magical. From the moment the bride and her father began their entrance down the grand staircase flanked by beautiful vineyards  through the lovely ceremony to the signature drinks on the patio culminating with a fairytale like setting in the beautifully draped tent. I've been to weddings in the Livermore Valley, the Napa Valley, the Mediterranean coast of Santa Margarita, Italy, and I have to say that the warmth of the staff and the ambience of Nella Terra place it at the top of my list.

Follow on Instagram @nellaterra and you'll see that my words fall short. The photos are beautiful. I’m so impressed of late with the adaptations for Covid World small, intimate yet safe and socially distanced weddings. There are so many venue sites for the ceremony and myriad sites for spectacular wedding photos.The grounds are so expansive, social distancing for a large group seems quite doable. At 71,years of age, I still find joy in seeing everything from creative seating charts to tables scapes and floral arrangements. We’re fortunate to have this gem in the East Bay.

Nella Terra is a beautiful, unique and special venue. I recommend it highly.</text>< Pics>

<Review>Great spot! Great wine!
My husband and I attended the most beautiful wedding at Nella Terra! Our friends were lucky to find this hidden gem so close to home. The amazing venue has scenic overlooks, intimate walks, and beautiful landscaping perfect for any size wedding and every picture you and your guests could dream of taking!

It has been a year since my husband and I flew from Texas to California for Ty and Whitney’s wedding and I wanted to post this here in honor of their anniversary. When we were dropped off at the venue, we had a lovely walk through the vineyard to the wedding location. The views of the countryside, the vineyard, the wedding site and the reception tent were stunning.  We were surrounded by beauty. We were able to socialize with a glass of wine under the pergola before the start of the ceremony which was such a lovely concept. Then, we were seated for the wedding in the sunny open air that only California can deliver. After the ceremony, we enjoyed several appetizer stations placed throughout the area where chefs were preparing their specialty on site. You also had time to stroll around the grounds and take in all its’ beauty. Entering the reception tent was truly magical. The table décor, flowers, and personal place settings were exquisite and the attention to detail was impeccable. The wedding at Nella Terra was absolutely the most beautiful wedding I have ever attended, and it is a memory I will treasure forever.<//review>

I can't say enough great things about Nella Terra Cellars. The venue is an oasis hidden in the Sunol rolling hills with a beautiful garden, mini waterfalls, fountains, romantic lighting, delicious wine and tented area with gorgeous lighting!

< Review>
My husband and I got married about a year ago at Nella Terra, and we continue to be in awe at the BEAUTY, UNIQUENESS, KINDNESS OF STAFF, and of course all the magical moments we had while celebrating our marriage that Nella Terra helped make possible.

When my husband and I started our wedding venue shopping, we were looking for a venue that represented California, had the capacity of being able to accommodate our large wedding party/guests, and full of natural beauty. We quickly learned that Nella Terra hit all these points for us, and so many more.

First off, Nella Terra is an absolute diamond of a wedding venue and offers the whole package. It is truly a hidden gem, nestled in the rolling golden CA hills (which was a must have on my husband’s list). The grounds are absolutely stunning, and truly picturesque, there are so many beautiful photography spots. We loved how the ceremony site was only a few steps away from the reception area, and the gazebo for cocktail hour is a great place for all your guests to enjoy a glass of wine or beer before the reception starts! As the bride, one of my favorite things about Nella Terra is the grand cascading staircase. It makes for the perfect entrance to the beginning of such a breathtaking and magical wedding day. I continue to cherish that moment walking down the staircase, taking the whole venue in and seeing all our wedding plans come to life.

A few other items that we would like to mention:
The benefit of having the option for “indoor” and outdoor. Having the large tent for the reception could be used for the ceremony if weather doesn’t cooperate. Even though the venue is quite large, having a smaller more intimate wedding, particularly during social distancing times would be absolutely beautiful and would still be able to provide you with the same beautiful and magical wedding day experience that you are dreaming of. There is TONS of parking for all your guests.  The bridal cottage is so cute, and a fun place for the bride and all her gals to hangout in before the big moment!

The Catering company that Nella Terra uses is stellar! Loved working with On the Vine catering. From the moment of signing our wedding contract with Nella Terra, to the tasting and then having our menu come to life on our wedding day was flawless! We had so many complements from our guests! We really liked that you could do a dual entrée, so guests could have a plated dinner and receive both salmon and steak. We liked that the decision for a catering company was already decided for us, takes the headache out of researching and booking a company. We thoroughly loved the food and would highly recommend!

We cannot say enough about the Nella Terra Staff; very professional, responsive, and accommodating to certain questions and requests my husband and I had. We loved that Nella Terra made us feel like family and there were so many personal touches that made us feel special. Thank you to Whitney, Kendall, and Sharde for all their hard work that helped make our day super special and flawless and all other Nella Terra staff working behind the scenes.

This review wouldn’t be complete without mentioning their wine. Absolutely delicious, and there are many varieties to choose from! We are big pinot noir fans, and their wine does not disappoint!  We are proud Nella terra wine club members and look forward to swinging by the winery to pick up our quarterly shipments, it is a way for us to enjoy the grounds and the beauty that Nella Terra offers.  Not to mention reliving our wedding day each time we pick up our wine shipment.

So, you must add Nella Terra to your list of venues to visit, and if you are like us, will quickly realize it is a one of a kind wedding venue!</Review>

The family that owns and runs Nella Terra are often out mingling in the tasting room, which is so fun! I love bringing my family and friends up to enjoy the views and the delicious offerings when they are visiting from out of town. Pack a picnic and stop by to enjoy their wines - you will not be disappointed!

Events - first off, what a beautiful venue! It really is a rare gem in this area. Upon entering this venue you feel like you are so far away from the hustle of the near by cities, yet you are close enough to the freeway to make this venue completely accessible. From a wedding guests stand point - the venue team made sure everything went off seamlessly and my experience was 10/10. The ceremony and reception areas are separated but very close together, which eliminates the dreaded traveling in heels across long distances to get from place to place. You’ll find yourself surrounded by rolling hulls, big trees, flowering plants and so many vines!
It is a unique, clean, beautiful property.

<rate>1<//rate><Text>I'm writing as a very disappointed groom-to-be, and feel compelled to warn any couples from booking their wedding with Nella Terra. While we were impressed with the physical venue, we are livid with how Nella Terra and their required wedding coordinator, Simply Lovely, are treating couples impacted by COVID19. In this environment their business practices are downright shameful.

For some background, we paid a significant premium to have our wedding scheduled for a Saturday evening in early June. Due to the 'shelter in place' order, we've been completely unable to continue planning our wedding, as all the contractors and businesses we need to work with, in addition to Nella Terra, are closed. So those businesses providing our tuxes and scheduled fittings, my fiancé's and bridesmaids wedding dresses, caterers, entertainment etc. are all strictly shut down.

To make things worse, Nella Terra has been a nightmare to work with throughout this ordeal. Initially, they downplayed the seriousness of the crisis and ignored our concerns stating there would be no problem having the wedding in early June. As the crisis worsened and California instituted a lockdown, they seemed to better understand the severity of the crisis. Now with an early June wedding an impossibility, they are unwilling to reschedule us for the equivalent of what we have contracted for, which is a Summer Saturday wedding.

Our contract clearly states that in the event of an Act of God, Nella Terra will reschedule pending availability at no penalty. Since their Saturday schedule is booked thru Thanksgiving 2020, while it is not ideal, a postponement of our wedding another year to the Summer of 2021 would be a solution to at least consider. We requested to move our rescheduled wedding date to one of the many Saturdays they have open in Summer 2021, and were completely denied any of those open dates. They informed us this would be a loss of future revenue to them.

The owners' correspondence has been quite callous, adding insult to our complete disappointment. Due to their lack of willingness to provide us what we contracted for, we requested a refund. The owners literally scoffed at us while refusing to even listen to our situation. They were quick to enforce the part of the contract that states there will be no refunds, but refuse to honor the part that states we can reschedule pending availability with no penalty.

We paid for a Saturday Summer wedding and it's important to us to have something similar, as most of our guests are traveling from out of state. Nella Terra has repeatedly refused to allow us to reschedule for a Saturday that is open on their current calendar, instead only offering us Monday through Thursday options in 2021. We would never have contracted with them for a weekday wedding.  They also refuse to refund the difference in price from a premium weekend to weekday. Their reasoning is those weekend dates are reserved for new clients only, because they need to think about the health of their business and prices are increasing in 2021. If we want to move our date to a Saturday next summer, we would have to forfeit all current payments (~$24K) and then pay the increased 2021 price. How is this not profiteering and/or extortion?

It's clear to us Nella Terra is only concerned with making sure they don't miss a single cent of revenue opportunity, while cheating their current clients out of what they've paid for. We feel held hostage given we've paid almost the entire sum for the wedding. My fiancé is understandably devastated, given how much she's put into planning this wedding for over a year now. To be taken advantage by a business trying to profit off a world health crisis has us at a loss for words. The owners at Nella Terra should be ashamed of themselves.<//Text>< Pics>

<date>1458169306894<//date><GmapID>0x808fc3ff763523cb:0xbd3314d79738a6f5</GmapID><Pictures>None<//Pictures><rate>4<//rate><UserId.>102256588997957643557<//UserId.><Text>This review is from the viewpoint of a wedding attendee. Last weekend I had the honor of attending a beautiful wedding at this picturesque location.

Not the easiest place to find, but there are marked signs here and there. Note that there are NO street lights at night. Be careful of nice shoes as parking lot isn't paved. After walking what seems like endless # of steps to get to the seating area, it was worth it. The alter sits in front of a pond-like setting with a small bridge. Since it was a hot day, cold lemonade and ice water await in the back.

Cocktail hour and reception were held in the court yard and in a big open tent. Light breeze flowed through with some shade here and there outside. Cheerful staff members passed around light appetizers. I enjoyed the cucumber salmon bites and the crispy triangles. The hosts included an open bar so of course I had to try the wine.

Staff was well trained and dinner was brought out simultaneously for the 150 guests. Options included salmon, duck, steak, or vegetarian, which was pre-selected when I RSVP'ed. I forgot that I had gotten the duck that I felt was too salty. However, I really enjoyed the mashed potatoes because it was seasoned well, light and fluffy. I had a bite of the salmon and vegetarian dish, both were better than the duck in my opinion. No real kitchen on site, everything was prepped in a trailer?

FYI: No real restrooms on site. The restroom is an upscale potty in a trailer. Lots of air fresheners and vents inside, so smells were masked. Ladies, be careful walking up the metal steps because there are small holes on the metal that might get your heel stuck.

The night ended with lots of photo-booth action and dancing. The hosts hired a live band and the acoustics in the tent was just right. Night time became chilly, but dancing kept me warm. Overall, I would consider having a wedding here.<//Text><user_name>Jean L< /user_name><Response>None<//Response></record></dataset><record>
